Archives GAUQUELIN Return

Archives GAUQUELIN. 20663 Names of Successful Professionals
(All Data from Birth Certificate)
© CURA, ed. by Patrice Guinard : February 2009
 

BIRTH AND PLANETARY DATA GATHERED SINCE 1949
(Coordonnées natales et planétaires rassemblées depuis 1949)

These 20663 names of successful professionals, published in series A, D and E by Michel and Françoise Schneider-Gauquelin are in fact 20433 : 230 of them are doubles, but c. 800 are missing. For example the birth data of Émile Zola has been published in vol. A6 as writer and in vol. E3 as politician.
 

How to find the hour of birth of a professional in the Archives GAUQUELIN ?

1. Look at your name in this file. For example, the French historian of philosophy Émile Bréhier. Copy it without accents.

2. He is present as writer (WR) in volume 6 of the series A (A6). Check in a dictionary if it's the good one (born 12 April 1876), and go to the right file (902gdA6y.html). [There are 5 Henri or Henry Martin in the database].

3. Copy the year, month and day (as they are in the table "Chronological order with names") : 


1876	4	12

4. Paste them and find the complete data in the first table. 

1876	4	12	W	146	F	2	39	20	0	48N46	5E10	55	BAR-LE-DUC

 

Codes of Professions

Actors (AC) [including Pop Singers]
Artists (AR)
Executives (EX)
Journalists (JO)
Military Man (MI)
Musicians (MU)
Painters (PA)
Politicians (PO)
Scientists, Physicians (SC)
Sports Champions (SP)
Writers (WR)
various (X)
